		"slot_engineer_fists"
		{
//	COMMENT: Fun and useful trick here!
//			 You can equip two weapons at once on the loadout screen, with some caveats.
//			 In RR, if Engineer is using the full Army of Darkness set and completely runs out of ammo, he switches to his fists in his second melee slot!
//			 To achieve this, all Engineer melee's "bucket_position" params are set to "1", while the chainsaw's bucket position is set to "0". Engineer fists are also set to "bucket_position" "1".
//			 But the thing is: Engy's fists are also set as a "baseitem" in "item_slot" "utility".
//			 So, when a non-chainsaw melee is equipped, it doesn't allow access to the fists because of its bucket+bucket_position, because it's replaced!
//			 Finally, when the chainsaw is equipped, as well as having "bucket_position" "0", it allows the fists to be accessible!
//	DO NOTE: Mercs can't equip more than one of the same item_class! (important to know this!) If Engineer's fists were tf_weapon_wrench, then it prevents switching to it (on resupply/respawning)!
//	CAVEATS:
//		1) Can't equip more than one weapon item_class at a time (except tf_wearable, that one you can)
//		2) "bucket" has to be in the same slot as the extra weapon
//		3) Models in "utility" or "head" slots always show up in loadout screen
//		4) Must set "baseitem" to "1" (this spawns the player with the item by default)
//		5) Treat "bucket_position" as a second loadout slot

			"item_slot"					"utility"
			"bucket_position"			"1"
			"bucket"					"2"		//bucket could be set to 7 (making them inaccessible unless you run out of ammo), but that is just confusing.
		}
		"slot_heavy_get_fists_with_sandvich"
		{
// COMMENT: Same as above, but melee appears in melee subslot 0 instead of melee subslot 1
// Thing here is this prefab is only on the stock fists and not on all melees. There can only be one tf_weapon_fists, otherwise switching with resupply won't work.
			"item_slot"					"utility"
			"bucket_position"			"0"
			"bucket"					"2"
		}
